					<div class="post-title"><h3 itemprop="headline"><a href="https://ouispeakfashion.com/kseniaschnaider-unveils-fall-winter-2026/" title="KSENIASCHNAIDER Unveils Fall/Winter 2026 “Denim Workshop” — From Fabric to Concept">KSENIASCHNAIDER Unveils Fall/Winter 2026 “Denim Workshop” — From Fabric to Concept</a></h3></div>								<div class="post-content small">

					<div class="post-title"><h3 itemprop="headline"><a href="https://ouispeakfashion.com/alexander-wang-opens-new-cultural-hub-the-wang-contemporary-in-new-yorks-chinatown/" title="Alexander Wang Opens New Cultural Hub “THE WANG CONTEMPORARY” in New York’s Chinatown">Alexander Wang Opens New Cultural Hub “THE WANG CONTEMPORARY” in New York’s Chinatown</a></h3></div>								<div class="post-content small">
					<p>On February 20, New York–based fashion designer Alexander Wang and his mother, entrepreneur and philanthropist Ying Wang, officially opened a new cultural institution, “THE WANG CONTEMPORARY,” in New York’s Chinatown.</p>
					<footer class="post-links">

					<div class="post-title"><h3 itemprop="headline"><a href="https://ouispeakfashion.com/printings-jp-to-publish-0-0-10-an-archive-book-on-maison-martin-margiela/" title="printings.jp to Publish “0 0 10,” an Archive Book on MAISON MARTIN MARGIELA">printings.jp to Publish “0 0 10,” an Archive Book on MAISON MARTIN MARGIELA</a></h3></div>								<div class="post-content small">

					<div class="post-title"><h3 itemprop="headline"><a href="https://ouispeakfashion.com/bvlgari-appoints-dua-lipa-as-global-ambassador/" title="Bvlgari Appoints Dua Lipa as Global Ambassador">Bvlgari Appoints Dua Lipa as Global Ambassador</a></h3></div>								<div class="post-content small">
					<p>On February 19, the Italian luxury maison Bvlgari announced that it has appointed singer-songwriter Dua Lipa as its new Global Ambassador.</p>

	( function () {
		var completed = false;

		function initBreakpoints() {
			if ( completed ) {
				// This was fired already and completed no need to attach to the event listener.
				document.removeEventListener( 'DOMContentLoaded', initBreakpoints );
				return;
			}

			if ( 'undefined' === typeof window.tribe ) {
				return;
			}

			if ( 'undefined' === typeof window.tribe.events ) {
				return;
			}

			if ( 'undefined' === typeof window.tribe.events.views ) {
				return;
			}

			if ( 'undefined' === typeof window.tribe.events.views.breakpoints ) {
				return;
			}

			if ( 'function' !== typeof (window.tribe.events.views.breakpoints.setup) ) {
				return;
			}

			var container = document.querySelectorAll( '[data-view-breakpoint-pointer="3c0c23fa-9098-42f5-9c84-19391b190962"]' );
			if ( ! container ) {
				return;
			}

			window.tribe.events.views.breakpoints.setup( container );
			completed = true;
			// This was fired already and completed no need to attach to the event listener.
			document.removeEventListener( 'DOMContentLoaded', initBreakpoints );
		}

		// Try to init the breakpoints right away.
		initBreakpoints();
		document.addEventListener( 'DOMContentLoaded', initBreakpoints );
	})();

			<div class="post-title"><h3 itemprop="headline"><a href="https://ouispeakfashion.com/puig-2025-results-surpasses-e5-billion-for-the-first-time/" title="Puig 2025 Results: Surpasses €5 Billion for the First Time, Leading the Premium Beauty Market">Puig 2025 Results: Surpasses €5 Billion for the First Time, Leading the Premium Beauty Market</a></h3></div>						<div class="post-content">
			<p>Barcelona-based beauty and fashion group Puig announced its full-year and fourth-quarter 2025 results on February 18. Despite foreign exchange headwinds, the company maintained strong growth and surpassed €5 billion in annual revenue for the first time in its history.</p>
		</div>

			<p>On February 18, the British Fashion Council (BFC) announced the appointment of Clare Waight Keller, Creative Director of Uniqlo, and Kate Varah, Executive Director and Co-Chief Executive of the National Theatre, as new members of its Executive Board.</p>
